"A message from Mikey and Wewa"
"<p>Hello there! We are <span style=\"font-weight: bold\">Mikey and Wewa</span>
 and we create all kinds of stuff for TTRPG. Wewa hand-draws colorful 
battlemaps and assets, while Mikey writes adventures, creates monsters 
and rulebooks.</p><p>Thanks for your purchase and for supporting our 
work. We hope you will enjoy this map pack and create an awesome 
adventure with it. The map pack is play-ready, so just drag your players
 into one of the maps and enjoy your adventuring!<br></p><p>Few things:</p><ul><li>We've included several torches as tokens. They are on <b>Torches</b> page and you can easily drag and drop them into the <i>Dynamic Lighting</i>
 layer. They have various brightness and you should keep them on the 
Dynamic Lighting layer so the token will be hidden from players, but the
 light will be there.</li><li>We've used <span style=\"color: rgb( 255 , 0 , 0 )\"><b>red </b></span>for all the doors, but we use the little trick for doors in our games: use <span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"color: rgb( 0 , 255 , 255 )\">teal </span></span>for unlocked, <span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"color: rgb( 255 , 0 , 0 )\">red</span></span> for locked, and <span style=\"font-weight: bold\">black </span>or <span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><span style=\"color: rgb( 156 , 0 , 255 )\">purple </span></span>for arcane sealed, so you can easily keep track of what you prepared behind which doors.</li><li>Keep in mind that you can set <i>Dynamic Lighting</i> to some of your favorite settings, such as <b>Explorer Mode</b> and <b>Daylight mode</b>. We have set it to a \"vanilla\" setting, and you are free to tweak it to fit your needs!<br></li><li>Also, enjoy the night versions of the maps for some stealthy mission!</li><li>In this pack we included the Astral Sea Background, so your space sail can be even smoother!</li></ul><p>If you like our work, you can support us on <span style=\"font-weight: bold\"><a href=\"https://patreon.com/mikwewa\">Patreon</a></span>, where our patrons get maps and written stuff first, along with more awesome stuff we create.</p><p>We wish you fun gaming,</p><p>Mikey &amp; Wewa<br></p>"
"Vaclav"

"[GRE] Grenadier"
"<h1><span style=\"color: rgb( 8 , 82 , 148 )\">[GRE] GRENADIER</span></h1><p style=\"letter-spacing: normal\"><br></p><h3><span>Otoczeni zapachem tytoniu i prochu, ci hardzi gwardziści stanowią rdzeń niejednej drużyny. Na ramionach noszą ciężkie miotacze, przez barki przewieszone pasy amunicji, na grzbietach ciężkie pancerze kuloodporne, a w ustach okrzyki bitewne.
